1. I arrived at the hotel at 12:30 and asked to check in. I was told that I didn't have a room. I got angry and tried to solve the problem. I was embarrassed the whole time. The front desk supervisor didn't solve the problem and said that the rules had been written on the page and that check-in must be done at two o'clock! The original 13th floor was given to the 11th floor after I rejected the arrangement for the 5th floor, indicating that it can still be solved, but this attitude is bad!
2. The fruits provided in the room were very poor, and they also provided tea in a food stall bottle (I donâ€™t know who the person in charge chose this bottle, it is too ugly to be supplied by a hotel like this). He knocked on the door twice to disturb the guestsâ€™ rest, which was very annoying.
3. The air conditioning panel was out of control and I woke up from the heat in the middle of the night. Of course, I didnâ€™t want to look for the front desk in the middle of the night and wanted to rest. You can imagine the problem of air conditioning in summer...
4. The hotel added WeChat. I expressed the above opinions with the mentality of giving opinions, but... This is simply more unacceptable than the problem of the hotel itself. There was no follow-up after I raised the opinions.
5. There is a business package for booking a room. I called to ask for it, but the front desk didnâ€™t know. The restaurant was transferred to a Western restaurant. The Western restaurant said it was Chinese food. No one answered the call! No matter which depar**ent you are in, you represent the hotel, and you should actively handle and solve the guests' problems, and then
So the overall experience of staying at this hotel was not good.
